# Optimizing images and graphics: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

Optimizing images, icons & interactive elements
===============================================

When someone can’t see your site, whether they’re using a screen reader or their bandwidth is limited, the way you describe your images and icons become incredibly important.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When someone can’t see your site, whether they’re using a screen reader or their bandwidth is limited, the way you describe your images and icons become incredibly important.
==============================================================================================================================================================================

That’s where things like alt text and ARIA labels come in. They fill in the blanks for people who can’t rely on visuals, and they give search engines more context about what’s actually on the page. In this lesson, we’ll walk through how to describe visual and interactive elements using the right accessibility tools — like alt text for images, ARIA labels for icons, and clear, descriptive button and link text.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/BIUhS82TUg88E7IZp5J7XlNhf4.jpg?width=3840&height=2160)

# Structuring content with semantic tags: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

Structuring content with semantic tags
======================================

If search engines can’t figure out the structure of your page, they’re less likely to show it to the right people.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If search engines can’t figure out the structure of your page, they’re less likely to show it to the right people.
==================================================================================================================

That’s why using semantic tags matter — they help your content make sense, even without the visuals. In this lesson, we’ll look at how to structure your site properly using heading levels, text tags, and frame labels — so everything is clear, readable, and easy to understand for both people and search engines.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/6M3AcsWadNCPvC8c3oXO7FGlIhw.jpg?width=3840&height=2160)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

=============================================

Jumping between pages doesn’t have to feel jarring.
---------------------------------------------------

Jumping between pages doesn’t have to feel jarring.
===================================================

With Page Effects in Framer, we can add smooth transitions that make our sites feel more cohesive — almost more “app-like”. Your site flows from one page to the next. It’s a small touch that helps everything feel more like a product and less like a collection of separate pages. In this lesson, I’ll show you how to easy it is animate between pages in Framer.

# Intro to SEO & accessibility: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

Intro to SEO & Accessibility in Framer
======================================

Search engines don’t “see” your site the way people do.
-------------------------------------------------------

Search engines don’t “see” your site the way people do.
=======================================================

They rely on structure, tags, and metadata to figure out what your content is about—and how useful it might be to someone searching for it. In this course, we’re going to look at how accessibility and SEO work together, what they do behind the scenes, and how the decisions you make when designing and building your site can have a real impact on both.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/hfduItrFgVT8o37uZ4LORnz36mA.jpg?width=3840&height=2160)

# Using Events for nested interactions: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

##### Lesson available soon

We’re still working on this one. Subscribe to find out as soon as it is or check below for the available lessons.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/ubTfjCYZW9fz6PXTE3oZ3owR68.png)

##### Lesson available soon

We’re still working on this one. Subscribe to find out as soon as it is or check below for the available lessons.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/ubTfjCYZW9fz6PXTE3oZ3owR68.png)

[**Subscribe**](https://www.youtube.com/@framer)

Using Events for nested interactions in Framer
==============================================

Sometimes we end up with an interaction inside of a component that we need to trigger from outside of that component.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes we end up with an interaction inside of a component that we need to trigger from outside of that component.
=====================================================================================================================

Well a special type of interaction in Framer, called an “Event”, makes that possible. Events are essential variables for interactions, which let us bubble up interactions within a child component so they can be use in a parent component or overlay. In this lesson, we’ll explore a couple common examples of scenarios where Events save the day.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/q1pQxtb50biN2haW8EqLX5uzAaA.jpg)

**Lesson details**

[Mastering Animations and Interactions in Framer](https://www.framer.com/academy/courses/mastering-animations-and-interactions-in-framer)

[Remix Project](https://framer.link/o7j8PPQ)

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/q1pQxtb50biN2haW8EqLX5uzAaA.jpg)

**Lesson details**

[Mastering Animations and Interactions in Framer](https://www.framer.com/academy/courses/mastering-animations-and-interactions-in-framer)

==================================================

Components are the building blocks of any interactive site — and when you add animation to them, they become so much more than static pieces.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Components are the building blocks of any interactive site — and when you add animation to them, they become so much more than static pieces.

==============================================

Component variants are a powerful way to define different states for a single element.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Component variants are a powerful way to define different states for a single element.

# Creating parallax with Scroll Speed: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

Creating parallax with Scroll Speed in Framer
=============================================

If you’ve ever looked out the window of a moving car and noticed that the trees on the side of the road are whizzing by faster than the mountains in the distance, then you’ve observed something called "parallax".
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you’ve ever looked out the window of a moving car and noticed that the trees on the side of the road are whizzing by faster than the mountains in the distance, then you’ve observed something called "parallax".
====================================================================================================================================================================================================================

It’s a phenomenon we can exploit to make our brains _think_ that things are closer or further away. In this lesson, we’ll use Framer’s Scroll Speed effect to layer elements that move at different speed as the visitor scrolls, creating a sense of three dimensional depth.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/I77l4VsVuhDriINVIvWv3sVj3E.jpg?width=1920&height=1080)

# Transforming elements on scroll: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

Transforming elements on scroll in Framer
=========================================

Where Scroll Animations allowed us to \*trigger\* an animation that carried itself out with a pre-defined duration — Scroll Transforms let us translate scrolling into smooth, gradual changes to the position, scale, rotation, and opacity of an element.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Where Scroll Animations allowed us to \*trigger\* an animation that carried itself out with a pre-defined duration — Scroll Transforms let us translate scrolling into smooth, gradual changes to the position, scale, rotation, and opacity of an element.
===========================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Transforming elements on scroll lets the visitor drive, bringing a sense of connection between motion and input. It’s a super fun and powerful way to make your site feel more dynamic and reactive. In this lesson, we’ll look at how easy it is to make it happen in Framer.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/j5cUvq3CLtQp50X3Lb1gFkZNBPk.jpg?width=1920&height=1080)

# Triggering animations on scroll: Master UX & Web Design with free Framer Academy lessons

Triggering animations on scroll in Framer
=========================================

The Appear Effect is perfect for adding animations above the fold — since they start automatically when the page loads.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Appear Effect is perfect for adding animations above the fold — since they start automatically when the page loads.
=======================================================================================================================

But for elements further down the page, we might wanna wait to trigger animations until the visitor scrolls to a certain point. This is exactly where another effect called “Scroll Animations” come into play. In this lesson, we’ll look at how to trigger animations in Framer based on scroll position — from simple layer reveals to animating entire sections into view.

![](https://framerusercontent.com/images/oV5tjvLo25k1Iz6GxLeG1RVKbo.jpg?width=1920&height=1080)

# MCP — Framer Marketplace

MCP — Framer Marketplace

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Plugins](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/plugins/)

![Plugin icon](https://nw12xtr7iedsczg1le9s9pqfl.plugins.framercdn.com/icon.svg)

MCP
===

Bridge your Framer designs with AI assistants like Claude and Cursor. Edit text, update styles, create components, and export React code, all through natural language commands. One connection works across all your projects.

[Open in Framer](https://framer.com/projects/new?plugin=nw12xtr7iedsczg1le9s9pqfl)

[![Tommy D. Rossi](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcreators%2F29595%2Favatar-VnwsfFjinujsKl2PI83QMDayj7xiPw.jpg&w=48&q=90)\
\
Tommy D. Rossi\
\
Creator](https://www.framer.com/@unframer/)

1 week ago1w ago

Updated

5

Version

Free

Pricing

494

Users

![Screenshot 1 for MCP, a Framer Marketplace plugin by Tommy D. Rossi.](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fplugins%2F446-nlBg8NyAtIRHaRABqP6o52L6w3IXfJ&w=3840&q=100)

![Screenshot 2 for MCP, a Framer Marketplace plugin by Tommy D. Rossi.](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fplugins%2F446-9f1U6GZLPrS5pDdSbXhCESA7rK0dJQ&w=3840&q=100)

Connect your Framer projects to AI assistants using the Model Context Protocol (MCP). This plugin enables Claude, Cursor, and other MCP-compatible tools to directly interact with your Framer designs through a secure tunnel connection.

• Ask Claude to rewrite your landing page copy based on SEO research

• Create custom code components and insert them directly into your canvas

• Update color styles across your entire project with a single command

• Export Framer components as production-ready React code

• Automate design updates using AI-generated content

How It Works
------------

The plugin creates a secure WebSocket tunnel between your Framer project and MCP-compatible AI assistants. Your Framer user ID serves as a unique identifier, ensuring the connection remains consistent across all your projects.

When you make a request through Claude or another MCP client, it travels through a Cloudflare Worker to your open Framer plugin, where it executes using Framer's Plugin API. The response then returns through the same secure channel.

The MCP URL includes your user ID and an optional session secret for enhanced security. This URL remains the same across all your Framer projects, so you only need to configure it once.

Available Tools
---------------

• Project Structure - Get XML representation of pages, components, and code files

• Node Selection - Read and manipulate currently selected elements

• XML Updates - Modify node attributes, text content, and structure

• Color Styles - Create, update, and apply project color styles

• Text Styles - Manage typography styles with full property control

• Font Search - Find and apply fonts from Framer's font library

• Node Operations - Duplicate, delete, or zoom to specific nodes

• React Export - Convert Framer components to React code with [unframer CLI](https://github.com/remorses/unframer)
 (integrates with [React Export plugin](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/plugins/react-export/)
, shares the same [subscription](https://unframer.co/)
)

• Code Files - Create, read, and update TypeScript/React code components

• Component Insertion - Add components to canvas with proper positioning

Connecting to AI Assistants
---------------------------

Claude Desktop App:

1\. Open Claude Desktop settings (menu bar > Settings)

2\. Navigate to Developer tab > Edit config

3\. Add the MCP server URL from the plugin to your configuration

4\. Restart Claude Desktop to activate the connection

Cursor IDE:

1\. Open command palette (Cmd/Ctrl + Shift + P)

2\. Search for "Cursor Settings" and select MCP option

3\. Add the server configuration to ~/.cursor/mcp.json

4\. Refresh MCP servers in settings

5\. Use Cursor in agent mode to access MCP tools

Claude Code:

1\. Install Claude Code CLI (without sudo)

2\. Run: claude mcp add "framer-mcp" <your-mcp-url>

3\. The server will be available in all Claude Code sessions

Technical Details
-----------------

The system uses three components working together:

• Framer Plugin - Runs inside Framer, handles API calls and maintains WebSocket connection

• MCP Server - Cloudflare Worker implementing the MCP protocol at mcp.unframer.co

• WebSocket Tunnel - Bidirectional connection using your Framer user ID as identifier

Only one plugin instance can connect per user to prevent conflicts. Multiple MCP clients can connect simultaneously to the same plugin. All requests include a 5-second timeout for reliability.

The plugin supports request/response correlation via message IDs and implements automatic reconnection with exponential backoff. All tool operations are validated before execution to ensure design integrity.

Security Considerations
-----------------------

• Never share your MCP URL containing the session secret

• The connection is tied to your Framer user account

• All operations require explicit approval in your MCP client

• The plugin only has access to the currently open project

Example Workflows
-----------------

Landing Page Optimization:

Use Claude to research keywords, then ask it to update your page headings and meta descriptions with SEO-optimized content.

Design System Updates:

Ask Claude to create a consistent color palette and apply it across all components using color styles.

Component Development:

Build custom React components with Claude Code and insert them directly into your Framer project.

Content Migration:

Export existing components as React code and integrate them into your production application. The React Export feature integrates with the Framer React Export plugin—if you have an existing subscription, you can use it seamlessly with MCP.

Automated Testing:

Use MCP tools to verify all text styles follow accessibility guidelines and update non-compliant elements.

Saving space in the Framer canvas
---------------------------------

This plugin needs to always remain open to use MCP. To save space and not consume too much space you can click the collapse button in the bottom right of the plugin. This minimizes the plugin window.

Using Framer MCP programatically
--------------------------------

This MCP can be used also with tools to control Framer programatically for agentic tasks. For example you will be able create an agent that uses Framer to add new blog posts based on SEO keyword research

Velvera — Hair salon template
=============================

Velvera is a modern landing page template designed for hair salons, barbershops, and beauty studios. It helps businesses showcase their services, team, and customer reviews while making it easy for clients to book appointments

About this Template
-------------------

**What is Velvera & Who is it for?**

Velvera is a stylish and user-friendly landing page template made for hair salons and beauty professionals. It helps businesses present their services in a clean and engaging way while offering an easy way for customers to book appointments.

Ideal for salons, barbershops, and hairstylists looking for a professional online presence without the complexity of CMS

*   Problem & solution section to highlight common hair concerns and how the salon solves them
    
*   Services section to display all available treatments in a structured layout
    
*   About us section to share the salon’s mission, story, and uniqueness
    
*   Reviews & testimonials to build trust with real customer feedback
    
*   Team section to introduce hairstylists with their names and roles
    
*   Appointment & contact section for easy booking and direct communication
    
*   No CMS but properly set up sections for services and other important details

A11y Optimized

SoundToggle: Free Component by Kalim Khan — Framer Marketplace

![Component preview thumbnail](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcomponents%2FDWjsDdkn6RAFIHUqGQqm%2Fsoundtoggle-qLgi97XkUIkIShzQwaaF1vtZJBW6wT&w=1920&q=90)

SoundToggle
===========

A customizable sound toggle button that supports auto play and works smoothly across multiple browsers. Perfect for adding audio controls to your Framer projects with ease.

* * *

About this Component
--------------------

A fully customizable sound toggle built for Framer. It supports **auto play**, works across **all major browsers**, and gives you full control over the design and functionality.

**Key Features:**

*   Upload and control your own audio files
    
*   Autoplay support
    
*   Toggle sound on/off with smooth transitions
    
*   Customize icons, labels, and colors
    
*   Responsive and lightweight
    
*   Works seamlessly across multiple browsers
    

Ideal for adding background music or sound effects to your Framer sites.

* * *

About
-----

Confetti creates a fun particle animation system with realistic physics, featuring confetti pieces that fall, spin, and sway in the air. It can create both continuous rainfall and explosion effects.

This component a part of the 400+ components, layouts, templates, UI Kits and code overrides from SegmentUI PRO. Click [here](https://segmentui.com/uikit)
 to see the full library

Instructions
------------

1.  Copy and paste the component into your project file
    
2.  Choose between explosion mode or continuous fall by toggling the Explode property
    
3.  Customize the confetti's appearance and behavior through the properties panel (colors, size, speed, physics)
    
4.  For explosion effects, adjust the Explosion Delay and Distance to control the initial burst timing and spread
    

How It Works
------------

![](blob:https://www.framer.com/10c6ad4b-4f7d-48a6-ac71-4fff646299fc)

The component offers extensive customization through properties:

*   Explosion Settings: Control initial burst and timing
    
*   Z-Index Range: Manage depth layers for 3D effect
    
*   Colors: Customize confetti piece colors (up to 8)
    
*   Size/Speed: Adjust confetti dimensions and movement
    
*   Physics Properties: Fine-tune flip rate, sway, air drag
    
*   Density: Control number of confetti pieces
    
*   Length Factor: Adjust confetti piece shape

Progressify
===========

A fixed scroll progress bar that visually indicates how far a user has scrolled down the page.

![](https://y4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com/components/description-image-r9bzv5t7-W0AAJTH09ICqXXjA4diUQBkRHmMBuj)

Progressify – Visual Scroll Indicator for Your Pages
----------------------------------------------------

The Progressify component adds a sleek, fixed progress bar to the top or bottom of your page, giving users a clear visual cue of their scroll position. Customize its colors and position to match your brand and improve user experience on long pages.

Features:
---------

*   Customizable bar and container colors
    
*   Option to position at the top or bottom of the viewport
    
*   Smooth width animation for a polished feel
    
*   Automatically adapts to page height and scroll position
    
*   Preview-friendly with placeholder progress in the Framer editor
    

How it works:
-------------

Drop Progressify into your project, pick your colors and preferred position, and it’s ready to go—no extra setup or coding required.

Perfect for:
------------

*   Blogs and content-heavy pages
    
*   Landing pages and marketing sites
    
*   Portfolios and case studies
    
*   Any Framer project needing a subtle UX enhancement

About this Template
-------------------

The [**AI Startup Website Kit**](https://www.framer.com/free-ai-startup-kit)
 empowers you to effortlessly design and launch a fully functional, responsive, no-code website in just minutes. Packed with a variety of AI-inspired UI elements, this kit simplifies the process—just copy, paste, and build your page with ease.

Discover over **100 meticulously designed elements**, thoughtfully categorized into 15 groups to suit every purpose:

*   Example Pages
    
*   Headers
    
*   Features
    
*   Testimonials
    
*   Contact Forms
    
*   Companies
    
*   Pricing Tables
    
*   Changelog
    
*   Navigations
    
*   CTAs
    
*   404 Page
    
*   Buttons
    
*   3D Assets
    
*   Icons
    
*   Patterns
    
*   Typography

About this Component
--------------------

**Features:**

*   Adjustable **Shadow Offset**, **Blur**, and **Brightness**
    
*   Control **Tilt Intensity** for subtle or dramatic effects
    
*   Flexible **Height Mode** options (Fixed or Dynamic)
    
*   Works with PNG logos, images, and text
    
*   Smooth, responsive animations
    

**How to Use:**

1.  Import your PNG text, logo, or image (high-resolution recommended).
    
2.  Adjust shadow and tilt settings to your preference.
    
3.  Pick a height mode for your effect.
    
4.  Save and enjoy an engaging, interactive design element.

Masonry Gallery
===============

A smart, responsive masonry gallery with Pinterest-style layout and intelligent image placement. Ideal for portfolios & visual showcases.

* * *

About this Component
--------------------

Bring Pinterest-style layout magic to your Framer projects with this advanced Masonry Gallery component. Built with performance and customization in mind, it intelligently arranges your images using multiple layout algorithms, including:

*   **Balanced** (smart vertical distribution)
    
*   **Random** (chaotic aesthetic)
    
*   **Shuffled** (most balanced random)
    
*   **Sequential** (original order)
    

**Key features:**

*   Fully responsive column system
    
*   Hover animations and image overlays
    
*   Intelligent image height estimation for layout precision
    
*   An optional random seed for repeatable shuffles
    
*   Customizable gap, border radius, and more
    

**Perfect for:**

*   Portfolio grids
    
*   Case studies
    
*   Product displays
    
*   Moodboards and inspiration boards
    

Drop it into your Framer project, choose your layout style, and let the gallery do the heavy lifting.

About this Template
-------------------

**Nirvana** is crafted for spas looking to provide a luxurious and peaceful online experience.

Whether offering deep relaxation or beauty treatments, this template ensures a smooth, inviting, and high-converting presence💆‍♀️🌸

*   **Booking section** – effortless appointment scheduling for spa treatments
    
*   **Services display** – beautifully structured to highlight massages, facials, and therapies
    
*   **Reviews section** to showcase client experiences and build trust
    
*   Calming animations for a relaxing and premium feel
    
*   Fully responsive design for a flawless experience on any device
    
*   SEO-optimized to attract wellness seekers 🌍
    
*   Easy to customize and update without CMS
    
*   Free for all – perfect for any spa or wellness business

A11y Optimized

Animations & Effects

Automated SEO

Built-in Analytics

Project Styles

Slideshows/Tickers

About this Component
--------------------

QueryBox is a dynamic FAQ component built to make information easy to access. With a clean design, smooth toggles, and full responsiveness, it organizes your most common questions into a user-friendly experience. Fully customizable and simple to integrate, QueryBox helps your audience find answers faster while keeping your site looking modern and professional.

--------------------

*   **Built for Conversion:** A beautiful, intuitive rating system builds trust and drives engagement, helping you create designs that get results.

# Page Views: Premium Component by Nabeel — Framer Marketplace

Page Views: Premium Component by Nabeel — Framer Marketplace

![Component preview thumbnail](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcomponents%2FNCa7uK3PNft3xSJDaZkv%2Fpage-views-ANmZ8Nk9B2V2hIUg1f2mVTFAgZavPK&w=1920&q=90)

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Components](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/components/)

Page Views
==========

This component tracks and displays the number of visits to each page. It automatically increments and persists the view count across all visitors using a Supabase database

Purchase for $19

[![Nabeel](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcreators%2F29351%2FdpAI-XbLekovJheHW07MMGLXwmYTW0u3mgr.jpeg&w=48&q=90)\
\
Nabeel\
\
Creator](https://www.framer.com/@nabeel/)

3w ago

Updated

362

Views

[![Nabeel](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcreators%2F29351%2FdpAI-XbLekovJheHW07MMGLXwmYTW0u3mgr.jpeg&w=48&q=90)\
\
Nabeel\
\
Creator](https://www.framer.com/@nabeel/)

3w ago

Updated

362

Views

[Make it with Workshop\
\
Build your own component with AI](https://www.framer.com/workshop)

* * *

About
-----

This component tracks and displays the number of visits to each page. It automatically increments and persists the view count across all visitors using a Supabase database. No need for additional APIs/subscriptions/set up. Just drag and drop and see it in effect.

This component a part of the 400+ components, layouts, templates, UI Kits and code overrides from SegmentUI PRO. Click [here](https://segmentui.com/uikit)
 to see the full library

Instructions
------------

1.  Copy and paste the PageViews component code into your project file
    
2.  Add the component where you want to display the view count
    
3.  Customize the appearance through the properties panel:
    
    *   Set the suffix text
        
    *   Adjust the font settings
        
    *   Change the text color
        
4.  The counter will automatically start tracking views when published
    
    *   Note: In preview mode, you'll see a placeholder "123"
        
    *   The actual count appears only on the published site
        

How It Works
------------

![](https://y4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com/components/description-image-zw48grv7-ryeGJSPlapOPWueZWKnRCBGymsfdKm)

The component is pre-connected to a public Supabase database that tracks page views per URL automatically. You just need to copy and paste it on your page. The views are tracked based on the **URL of your published site.**

You can customize through property controls:

1.  Suffix: Text that appears after the number (e.g., "views", "visitors")
    
2.  Font: Complete typography control
    
3.  Text Color: Color of the counter text
    

**Note**: The component uses a shared public Supabase instance with rate limiting and row-level security in place. While this isn't the most secure approach, it enables drag-and-drop functionality since we're only tracking basic interactions.

Support
-------

For any queries and help setting up the component, contact [hello@segmentui.com](mailto:hello@segmentui.com)

About this Template
-------------------

As a cinematographer, director, or creative professional, having a portfolio that effectively showcases your work is essential. This template is designed with you in mind, providing an engaging and visually stunning platform to display your creative achievements.

The template is designed to make your work stand out with its captivating layout and attention-grabbing design. You can use it to showcase your best work and give your audience a glimpse into your creative vision and capabilities.

The template also includes various features to help you effectively organize and display your work. You can include detailed descriptions and information about each project and add multimedia elements such as videos and images to create a truly immersive experience for your audience.

With this template, you can showcase your work in a way that captivates your audience and helps you stand out from the crowd. Whether you’re a cinematographer, director, or creative professional, this template is the perfect platform to bring your work to life and take your career to the next level.

Angled Screen
=============

Makes screenshots less boring. Adjust viewing angles, add depth-of-field effects and apply film grain to give your images a more tactile, photographic quality.

[Open in Framer](https://framer.com/projects/new?plugin=jo5xt7kzua9ju0le4y7eiix8c)

About this Plugin
-----------------

Angled Screen transforms flat screenshots into eye-catching visuals by adding depth, perspective, and texture. This Framer plugin lets you adjust the viewing angle, apply subtle depth-of-field effects, and introduce film grain to give your images a more tactile, photographic quality.

Perfect for presentations, marketing materials, or portfolio work where standard screenshots feel too static. Play with the settings to find the sweet spot between subtle and striking, making your screen captures feel more like carefully composed photographs than simple grabs.

Changelog
---------

Version 4 • 3 months ago

*   Disable the image mode, only allow edit image and canvas, fix errors about plugin not being available for new image insertion
    
*   Compress the result image to make saving image step faster

Business Blog Website Templates
===============================

About this Template
-------------------

Embark on a creative expedition with Feedo, your dedicated companion in the realm of design. Feedo is poised to refine and elevate your creative journey, offering steadfast support to ensure your work radiates brilliance on every screen. Immerse yourself in a world of seamless and intuitive design, where Feedo transforms the ordinary into the extraordinary.

Meet Feedo: Your Guiding Light in the Creative Realm. In the dynamic landscape of design, Feedo takes center stage as your steadfast companion, committed to enhancing and refining your creative journey. With Feedo by your side, immerse yourself in a seamless and intuitive design experience that guarantees your work shines brilliantly on every screen. Let Feedo guide you to new heights of creativity and excellence.

# Image Masked Text: Free Component by Joseph Alexander — Framer Marketplace

Image Masked Text: Free Component by Joseph Alexander — Framer Marketplace

![Component preview thumbnail](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcomponents%2FQ2QaIrUFpWWlG3HMDsxi%2Fimage-masked-text-rRANSTP1FBXbge9BJblUYeT2j4y686&w=1920&q=90)

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Components](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/components/)

Image Masked Text
=================

Creates text with an image mask effect, allowing customizable fonts, image fitting options (cover/contain/percent), and fallback text color for striking typography.

Copy Component

[![Joseph Alexander](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcreators%2F30929%2Favatarme-huNfMRLO8tm6y99B5JhCTp23eziKSs.jpg&w=48&q=90)\

* * *

About this Component
--------------------

Creates visually striking text where an image appears inside the letter shapes using CSS masking techniques. The component clips background images to the text outline, making images visible only within the text characters.

**Key Features:**

**Text Masking:** Uses background-clip properties to create the mask effect, where the background image is only visible within the text shapes, creating dramatic visual typography.

**Flexible Image Fitting:** Offers three image fit options:

*   **Cover:** Image scales to cover the entire text area
    
*   **Contain:** Image scales to fit entirely within the text bounds
    
*   **Percent:** Custom scaling from 10% to 200% with center positioning
    

**Typography Controls:** Full font customization including size, weight, style, line height, letter spacing, and text alignment.

**Fallback Handling:** When no image is provided or fails to load, gracefully displays solid colored text using the specified text color, ensuring your design always works.

**Responsive Design:** Content automatically centers within its container and adapts to any layout dimensions, maintaining visual balance across different screen sizes.

Perfect for creating eye-catching headlines, hero text, or decorative typography where you want to fill text with textures, patterns, or photographic content while maintaining complete control over typography and layout. Ideal for landing pages, promotional materials, and artistic text treatments.

About this Template
-------------------

Eniwave combines sleek modern aesthetics with high functionality, offering a visually compelling space to showcase your work. Whether you’re a graphic designer, photographer, developer, or a creative team, this template’s bold yet minimalistic design ensures your content remains the focus.

Featuring seamless navigation, responsive layouts, and dynamic visuals, Eniwave allows your portfolio to shine across all devices. Its smooth transitions and subtle animations make your work stand out without distractions. Perfect for those looking to leave a memorable impression, Eniwave empowers you to build an engaging digital presence that not only captivates visitors but elevates your brand in today’s competitive market.

Unlock new possibilities with Eniwave and transform your portfolio into a dynamic showcase of innovation and creativity.

About this Template
-------------------

Introducing Educare, the ultimate Framer template designed to make your college or university website stand out. With 16 ready-to-use pages, you can build a stunning website faster than ever. Perfect for those who want a beautiful and functional site without the hassle.

From highlighting academic programs to introducing your dedicated faculty, Harbor makes it easy to present your school in the best light. Create a captivating online presence effortlessly with this versatile template.

**This Template is Best For:**

*   Colleges
    
*   Universities
    
*   School
    
*   Education Campus
    
*   Educational Institutions
    
*   Online Learning Platforms
    
*   Training Centers
    
*   Academic Conferences
    
*   Student Organizations
    

**Features:**

*   16 Ready to Use Pages
    
*   Multiple CMS Support
    
*   Advanced Form Builder
    
*   **Free Figma File**
    
*   Premium, clean, modern, and stylish design
    
*   Lifetime Support
    
*   Lifetime Update

About this Template
-------------------

This premium template is crafted for dance schools and teachers looking to build a captivating online presence. With its elegant and dynamic design, it highlights your classes, team, and success stories in a visually engaging way, making it easy to connect with potential students.

Designed for both style and functionality, the template features dedicated sections for class schedules, teacher bios, and testimonials, ensuring visitors get a clear and compelling introduction to your school. The fully responsive layout guarantees a seamless experience across all devices, while the intuitive navigation keeps engagement effortless.

Built on Framer, this template allows for complete customization, including colors, typography, layouts, and imagery, enabling you to create a website that truly represents your dance school’s brand and artistic vision. Whether you're launching a new school or refining your digital presence, this template provides the versatility and impact needed to attract and inspire students.

Make a powerful impression and bring the rhythm of your dance school to life with this beautifully designed template.

Draftr

Draftr — SaaS and Software Template
===================================

A fast and minimal Framer template designed for SaaS and software websites. Built for clarity, conversion and speed. Perfect for AI tools, digital products and startup landing pages that need a modern and clean layout.

A high-converting Framer template built for SaaS, software and AI product websites.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This template is perfect for founders, startups and digital product creators who want a simple and modern design that gets results. It features a clean layout, structured sections and strong typography to keep the focus on your product and drive signups.

The design is fully responsive, optimized for performance and easy to customize in Framer. Whether you are launching a SaaS, showcasing an AI product or building a software tool, this template helps you create a landing page that performs.

Key Benefits:

*   Purpose-built for SaaS, software, AI and digital product websites
    
*   Minimal layout with clear visual hierarchy and strong typography
    
*   Designed for conversion with focused call-to-action sections
    
*   Mobile-friendly, fully responsive across all screen sizes
    
*   Optimized for SEO and fast loading
    
*   Fully customizable in Framer without coding
    

Launch your software or SaaS product with a design that is clear, elegant and built to convert.

Ledger

Ledger — Clean template for B2B services
========================================

Ledger is a clean and versatile Framer template for B2B service-based businesses. Perfect for accounting, consulting, and financial services, it features a professional layout, CMS collections, and easy customization to build trust and showcase your offerings.

About this Template
-------------------

Ledger is a modern Framer template tailored to meet the needs of B2B service-based businesses. Whether you provide accounting, consulting, or financial management services, Ledger offers a clean, professional platform to showcase your expertise and build client trust. Designed with credibility in mind, it helps create an impactful first impression.

This template includes two CMS collections for services and a blog, making content management straightforward. It features a built-in contact form, customizable text and color styles, and a variety of drag-and-drop components to speed up your workflow. Subtle animations, page transitions, and an intuitive structure create a polished, engaging experience across all devices—helping you make a strong first impression.

About this Template
-------------------

Educate is a specialized Framer website template meticulously crafted for digital course creators. Designed with a comprehensive conversion funnel, it provides all essential tools to effectively market and sell your courses online. From captivating landing pages that engage visitors to seamless checkout processes that facilitate easy enrollment, Educate ensures every step of the customer journey is optimized for maximum conversions.

This template empowers educators to showcase their expertise with compelling content sections, interactive features, and intuitive navigation. Customizable and user-friendly, Educate allows you to personalize your site to reflect your brand identity while leveraging proven design elements that enhance user experience and drive sales.

Whether you’re launching a new course or scaling your educational offerings, Educate equips you with the framework to succeed in the competitive online education market. Transform your digital presence and engage learners with a professional and effective platform tailored for educational success.

About this Plugin
-----------------

**Easy Social Share - The Ultimate Framer Plugin for Effortless Sharing!** 🚀

Make social sharing seamless with **Easy Social Share**, a powerful **no-setup** Framer plugin designed to expand your content’s reach instantly! No API keys, no accounts—just simple, **one-click sharing** across **20+ social media platforms**.

✨ **Key Features:**

✅ **No API or Accounts Needed** – Works instantly, no complicated setup required.✅ **One-Click Sharing** – Easily share to Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, WhatsApp, and more.✅ **Automatic Integration** – Auto-adds share buttons to blog posts & pages.✅ **Built-in URL Shortening** – Keep links clean and shareable with automatic short URLs.✅ **Customizable Design** – Match your brand with adjustable styles and layouts.✅ **Mobile & Desktop Ready** – Optimized for all devices with deep-link support.✅ **Fast & Lightweight** – No extra load time, just smooth sharing.

Enhance your Framer projects with **Easy Social Share**—no coding, no hassle, just **effortless sharing**! 🚀

# FramerSync — Framer Marketplace

FramerSync — Framer Marketplace

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Plugins](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/plugins/)

![Plugin icon](https://cxmjflv066qj3p60chx5t4ufs.plugins.framercdn.com/icon.svg)

FramerSync
==========

Sync Notion, Airtable, and Google Sheets with the Framer CMS.

[Open in Framer](https://framer.com/projects/new?plugin=cxmjflv066qj3p60chx5t4ufs)

[![Isaac Roberts](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcreators%2F35028%2FkSFjV8bIu-AKT3u2pg7PrZL7rowyGEY3MFSLial5&w=48&q=90)\
\
Isaac Roberts\
\
Creator](https://www.framer.com/@framestack/)

2 weeks ago2w ago

Pricing

Users

![Screenshot 1 for FramerSync, a Framer Marketplace plugin by Isaac Roberts.](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fplugins%2F21-nBwERZD46PBZ1x4rRKwNhdukXY2L92&w=3840&q=100)

![Screenshot 2 for FramerSync, a Framer Marketplace plugin by Isaac Roberts.](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fplugins%2F21-ASWzxk16pMwryAtQ9mTCBVb15A524B&w=3840&q=100)

![Screenshot 3 for FramerSync, a Framer Marketplace plugin by Isaac Roberts.](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fplugins%2F21-FJJqBUbWfaws2P7wWU4PDugPxPvbzb&w=3840&q=100)

FramerSync does not have automatic syncing. If you need your collections to automatically sync, do not use this plugin.

Sync your data with the Framer CMS
----------------------------------

FramerSync connects Notion, Airtable, and Google Sheets with Framer, instantly importing all your content into the CMS and keeping it up-to-date. Use automation and formulas to generate data, generate programmatic SEO pages, manage your data outside of Framer, and keep all your team’s content in one place.You bring the content, FramerSync handles the rest.

How it works:
-------------

1.  Connect your Notion, Airtable or Google Sheets account
    
2.  Select a database to sync
    
3.  Configure CMS fields
    
4.  FramerSync imports your data instantly!
    

One-click sync
--------------

After you’ve connected your account and set up a CMS collection, you can sync your collection with new and updated content with just one click.

Work with your team
-------------------

If you’re working in a Framer project with team members, they can sync CMS collections too. Anyone with access to the project can sync, manage, and add new synced collections, just like they would with a regular non-synced CMS collection.

Packed with easy-to-use importing tools
---------------------------------------

FramerSync is loaded with tools for importing data. Here’s a few of them:

*   Import everything from Notion databases: page content, cover images, page icons, and every property type.
    
*   You choose which data to sync. Just uncheck a field in the plugin to stop it from being imported.
    
*   Import Markdown or HTML text from Google Sheets as Formatted Text in Framer - complete with headings, bold, italics, links, images, and all other formatting options.
    
*   Import fields with multiple items as multiple CMS fields. Framer CMS fields can’t have more than one value, so FramerSync converts fields with multiple values into multiple CMS fields in Framer. For example, a file field in Airtable with 3 files will be imported as File 1, File 2, and File 3.
    
*   And so much more!
    

Privacy and security
--------------------

FramerSync only gets access to the Notion databases, Airtable tables and Google Sheets you choose to share. These databases are only accessed when you open the plugin to sync or edit your collections, and are never stored on our servers.

Changelog
---------

Version 12 • 2 weeks ago

Fixed image and file arrays being cleared after re-syncing content from Notion.

AnimaType
=========

A versatile Framer component that creates a captivating visual effect by using an animated GIF as a background fill for text.

About this Component
--------------------

The component offers comprehensive customization options for typography, shadows, and strokes, allowing for a wide range of creative applications. It also includes a robust loading state to ensure a smooth user experience while the GIF is being fetched.

Features

*   **Animated Text Fill** - Uses a GIF to dynamically fill text characters.
    
*   **Customizable Typography** - Adjust font family, size, weight, and text transformation.
    
*   **Text Effects** - Add and customize text shadows and strokes (outlines).
    
*   **Flexible Sourcing** - Use a GIF from a URL or upload your own GIF file.
    
*   **Responsive Scaling** - The component's bounding box correctly scales with the text.
    
*   **Full Framer Control Panel Integration** - All properties are adjustable directly in the Framer sidebar.
    
*   **Position and Rotation Control** - Easily position and rotate the component on the canvas.

About this Template
-------------------

Build your online brand with a website template that’s fast, powerful, and designed for creators like you. Publish your blog, sell your products, and grow your affiliate business – all with a sleek, mobile-first website that includes 10 ready-to-use pages, built-in dark/light mode, and smooth interactions.

It's easy to customize and has built-in native Framer forms. This template gives you everything you need to launch and scale your digital business quickly as a solopreneur.

About this Component
--------------------

**Fully Customizable Icons**  
Add up to 20 custom icons, graphics, or elements using the child system for complete creative control.  
  
**Advanced Animation Options**  
Choose from multiple fade types (linear, pop, instant) with configurable speed presets and scale animations for engaging visual effects.  
  
**Performance Optimized**  
Efficient animation loop with proper cleanup, bounds checking, and static rendering support ensures smooth performance across all devices.  
  
**Refund Policy**  
Due to the digital nature of my product, all sales are final, and refunds will not be issued. If you have any questions or need clarification, feel free to reach out before completing your order.  
  
[**hello@8ighty8.studio**](mailto:hello@8ighty8.studio)

About this Template
-------------------

**Archio** is a premium Framer template designed for interior designers, renovation agencies, and home improvement studios looking to showcase their work with sophistication.

Crafted with a clean aesthetic and smooth interactions, Archio helps you build trust, highlight past projects, and convert visitors into clients — without writing a single line of code.

Whether you're a solo designer or an established firm, Archio gives you the structure, style, and polish to launch fast and look professional.

**Key Features:**

*   Stunning portfolio layout with testimonials
*   Smooth animations and responsive design
*   FAQ, services, and contact sections ready to go
*   Easily customizable in Framer’s visual editor
*   Optimized for conversions and mobile performance

Perfect for:Interior Designers • Home Renovators • Architecture Studios • Freelancers

# Apex Charts — Framer Marketplace

Apex Charts — Framer Marketplace

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Plugins](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/plugins/)

![Plugin icon](https://7ybkj5h7a4wbiqi2b4oiga9e7.plugins.framercdn.com/icon.svg)

Apex Charts
===========

Use this no-code tool to enhance your app with Apex Charts. This plugin supports a wide range of features and customizations. Visualize data with customizable charts and interactive elements.

Take Your App to the Next Level with Apex Charts
------------------------------------------------

Enhance your app with the Apex Charts Plugin, a no-code solution for integrating customizable and interactive charts. This plugin allows you to create stunning data visualizations with ease, making it perfect for dashboards, reports, financial tracking, and more. Whether you're building a business analytics tool, an educational platform, or a financial app, Apex Charts provides the tools you need to transform raw data into clear, engaging visuals.

Key Features:
-------------

✅ **Custom Chart Styles**

*   Personalize chart colors, fonts, and layouts to match your app’s branding.
    

✅ **Multiple Chart Types**

*   Line charts, bar charts, area charts, pie charts, and more to fit any data visualization need.
    

✅ **Dynamic Data Updates**

*   Seamlessly update charts in real time as data changes.
    

✅ **Interactive Elements**

*   Enable tooltips, zoom, and hover effects for a richer user experience.
    

✅ **Smooth Performance**

*   Optimized rendering ensures fast loading and seamless interactions.
    

Empower your app with Apex Charts’ advanced capabilities and deliver insightful, professional-grade data visualizations to your users!

Start creating stunning visuals effortlessly today!

About this Component
--------------------

ParticleText FX is an animated typography system that turns words into vibrant particle formations. Each letter is made of hundreds of particles that move with natural physics - forming, dissolving, and reforming into new words with smooth transitions.

Animated text grabs attention instantly. ParticleText FX adds personality and interactivity to words, making your message not just seen - but felt.

**Features:**

*   **Text Formation** – smooth particle animations forming letters.
    
*   **Word Cycling** – auto-transitions between multiple words.
    
*   **Color Transitions** – vibrant word-by-word color blending.
    
*   **Advanced Physics** – velocity, acceleration, friction, force limiting.
    
*   **Customizable** – words array, font size, weight, draw style.

About this Template
-------------------

Perfect for content-heavy websites, NewsFlash combines flexibility and speed with a fully responsive layout across all devices. Whether you're launching a new website or refreshing an existing one, this modern template gives you everything you need to present your content without writing a single line of code.

*   **Optimized for Speed:** Fast load times and seamless navigation.
    
*   **Fully Responsive:** Perfectly adapts to all devices.
    
*   **SEO Ready:** Fully optimized for search engines.
    
*   **Modern Design:** Showcase your content beautifully.
    
*   **CMS Integration:** Easily manage your content via the CMS.
    
*   **Quick Setup:** Just add your content and hit publish—it's that simple!

----------------------

*   A high-converting landing page layout

Country Flags
=============

Consistently designed country flags in one app.

[Open in Framer](https://framer.com/projects/new?plugin=cu6e195tt0tjs4i8tbvuluhow)

About this Plugin
-----------------

We know flags all look different. Country Flags provides you a consistent set of flag designs, making everything feel cohesive.

Vibe

Vibe — DJ & Club Website Template
=================================

Vibe is a sleek, modern Framer template designed for DJs, featuring a dark aesthetic and customizable components to effectively showcase your music and events.

About this Template
-------------------

Vibe is a dark, modern template crafted specifically for DJs and music artists who want to stand out online. With its sleek design and over 10 customizable components, Vibe provides a platform to showcase your music, upcoming events, and connect with your audience seamlessly. The template includes 2 CMS collections, allowing for easy management of your content. Responsive and SEO optimized, Vibe ensures your website looks great on all devices and ranks well in search engine results, helping you reach a wider audience. 

**Main Features:**

*   **Modern Landing Page**: Captivate visitors with a sleek and engaging homepage.
    
*   **10+ Components**: Customize various sections to reflect your unique style.
    
*   **2 CMS Collections**: Easily manage your music and events content.
    
*   **Responsive & SEO Optimized**: Ensures optimal performance across devices and search engines.
    
*   **Event Listings**: Keep your audience informed about upcoming performances.
    
*   **Contact Form**: Facilitate easy communication with potential clients and fans.

# Save Image — Framer Marketplace

Save Image — Framer Marketplace

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Plugins](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/plugins/)

![Plugin icon](https://3pq88gxd8dv2ogptbhm8pr3lc.plugins.framercdn.com/icon.svg)

Save Image
==========

Download and copy images from your Framer project to reuse, move, or backup your images. Select any frame, component, or CMS collection to quickly save images.

[Open in Framer](https://framer.com/projects/new?plugin=3pq88gxd8dv2ogptbhm8pr3lc)

Save Images in Framer
---------------------

Quickly and easily download or copy images. This plugin enables you to reuse, move, or backup unlimited images in your projects.

The Save Image plugin is fully compatible with images in frames, component variables, CMS items, and any other images in Framer, so you can save images without limits.

*   100% free - no payment needed for unlimited usage.
    
*   Export at full resolution - no downscaling or resizing.
    
*   Simple and easy to use - select an image and download or copy with a single click.
    

Open-Source
-----------

You can find the full source code of this plugin on GitHub at [github.com/madebyisaacr/framer-save-image](https://github.com/madebyisaacr/framer-save-image)

Changelog
---------

Version 2 • 1 month ago

*   Added gallery fields support in CMS view

# Blog Side Nav (CMS): Premium Component by Dan Marek — Framer Marketplace

Blog Side Nav (CMS): Premium Component by Dan Marek — Framer Marketplace

![Component preview thumbnail](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcomponents%2FnVEu7ErMudPMgy0Vn7GS%2Fblog-side-nav-cms-bHiiVx9LbpJ46KCuiLqM8aytcyWOMB&w=1920&q=90)

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Components](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/components/)

Blog Side Nav (CMS)
===================

A dynamic table of contents component that updates seamlessly based on your page — and works with CMS!

Purchase for $5

[![Dan Marek](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcreators%2F28940%2F6d0MJdcJf21RQ6wMHwqlIhnIjvc-S4CurXlBHerBb9gilLBCgkpxiqogUC.png&w=48&q=90)\

\

[Make it with Workshop\
\
Build your own component with AI](https://www.framer.com/workshop)

* * *

About this Component
--------------------

Simply add this vertical Side Nav component to your website to instantly see a Dynamic Table of Contents that live updates based on the content on your site (even works for CMS content).  
  
Choose from two different modes:

1.  **Popover (inspired by Notion).** When you need to display extensive navigation in a clean, organized way, popover mode reveals a beautiful menu overlay on hover. Perfect for long-form content, documentation, or any situation where you want to show the complete content structure without cluttering your design.
    
2.  **Animated Lines (inspired by Stripe).** Perfect for minimal, focused navigation experiences. When users hover over navigation elements, lines dynamically scale based on proximity to their cursor, creating an elegant visual hierarchy that feels both sophisticated and intuitive.Watch the demo video to see these in action.
    

You have complete flexibility to choose what is shown inside the component and even create custom labels overrides too!

[View the full demo here](https://framer-toc-side-navigation.framer.website/dynamic-side-navigation-table-of-contents-component)

Framer Side Navigation Demo

# Smart Copyright: Free Component by Andreu — Framer Marketplace

Smart Copyright: Free Component by Andreu — Framer Marketplace

![Component preview thumbnail](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcomponents%2FQ8sxmTkcG0TlWSYtaQCy%2Fsmart-copyright-R7XGaZ5qm27WEYVkAuTfOWwo3ma37n&w=1920&q=90)

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Components](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/components/)

Smart Copyright
===============

An auto-updating copyright label with customizable name, symbol, and styling.

Copy Component

About this Component
--------------------

The Smart Copyright component is a dynamic and customizable Framer code component designed to streamline the process of displaying a professional copyright notice on your site. It automatically updates the year to reflect the current one, eliminating the need for manual edits every new calendar year.

Properties
----------

*   Name
    
*   Show ©
    
*   Show Name
    
*   Prefix / Suffix
    
*   Text Color
    
*   Font

Structora is a professionally designed Framer template specifically created for businesses in the interior design and architecture, interior, renovation, and building industries. It offers a range of features and customization options to cater to companies involved in interior and architecture-related services.

Structora includes 11 unique pages that helps you build a modern website within days, not weeks!

Whether you're a freelancer or agency owner, this template caters to your specific needs, offering seamless integration with multiple CMS platforms and an advanced form builder for effortless interaction with your audience.

About this Template
-------------------

JULES JOURNEY is a sleek, minimalist Portfolio Template designed specifically for AI Artists, Photographers, and Designers. Elegantly showcase your work with a stunning portfolio gallery, fully powered by the Framer CMS. Featuring custom cursors, horizontal scrolling, and dynamic page transitions, Jules Journey takes full advantage of Framer's capabilities.

--------

A11y Optimized

Animations & Effects

Automated SEO

Built-in Analytics

Light & Dark Theme

Overlays & Modals

Project Styles

Sticky Scrolling

About this Template
-------------------

Transform your investment firm's digital presence with this premium Framer template specifically designed for modern finance and climate-focused ventures. Clarity GV delivers a sophisticated yet accessible platform that communicates complex investment strategies with precision and impact.

The template features strategically structured sections that showcase your portfolio companies, investment thesis, and sustainability initiatives through a clean, professional aesthetic that builds immediate trust with potential partners and clients.

Key features include:

*   Customizable valuation calculator to boost engagement.
*   Advanced CMS with filtering allows you to share your Portfolio and sectors of expertise.
*   Interactive testimonial blocks.
*   Modern typography and spacing that ensures optimal readability across devices.
*   Expertly-crafted animations.
*   Apple-style interactive forms.

Bonuses:

*   SEO optimised to get you to the first page of Google.
*   Includes a simple style-guide to get you started.

Whether you're launching a new venture capital firm, refreshing your investment company's brand, or creating a compelling case for climate-focused finance, Clarity GV provides the versatile framework needed to convert visitors into partners without complex design requirements.

Built with conversion in mind, every element has been carefully crafted to balance professional authority with approachable communication, helping you launch faster and grow more effectively in the competitive investment landscape.

About this Template
-------------------

Refined, aspirational, and timeless—The Aether Studio Framer template is the ultimate solution for luxury architecture studios and developers who want to make a lasting impression. Designed with elegance and performance in mind, this template provides the perfect platform to showcase your studio’s visionary designs and architectural masterpieces. Its high-converting structure ensures your work captivates the most discerning clients, setting your brand apart as a leader in sophistication and innovation. Whether you’re unveiling iconic projects or introducing bold new concepts, The Aether Studio Framer template elevates your online presence to match the timeless quality of your craft.

# Copyright Notice: Free Component by figma2framer — Framer Marketplace

Copyright Notice: Free Component by figma2framer — Framer Marketplace

![Component preview thumbnail](https://www.framer.com/creators-assets/_next/image/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fy4pdgnepgswqffpt.public.blob.vercel-storage.com%2Fcomponents%2FWefwNQ2CXD81LqxwQMmk%2Fcopyright-notice-ADmW1zR8PKmufbkPwELtb7e5NQPqfd&w=1920&q=90)

[Marketplace](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/)
[Components](https://www.framer.com/marketplace/components/)

Copyright Notice
================

Auto-updating copyright notice with customizable symbol, name, year range, and link — ideal for any footer.

Copy Component

About this Component
--------------------

This component gives you a perfectly styled, auto-updating copyright text for footers — complete with legal symbols, date range, company name, and a privacy link.

**Features:**

*   Symbols
    
*   Date Range
    
*   Company Name
    
*   Company Statement
    
*   Suffix Text
    
*   Text Color Style
    
*   Font Styles
    
*   Text Alignment
    
*   Fill Width Control
    
*   Link
    
*   Link Text
    
*   Link URL
    
*   Link Style
    
*   Open in New Tab

About this Template
-------------------

Elevate your SaaS startup's online presence with our comprehensive Framer template. This versatile template includes multiple home page options (Home V1, Home V2), pricing page variations (Pricing V1, Pricing V2), and essential pages like About Us, Contact Us, Integrations, Blog, and Blog Article. Additionally, it covers all necessary legal documentation with Terms & Conditions and Privacy Policy pages. Featuring sleek design, seamless CMS integration, and top-tier performance, this template is your all-in-one solution to captivate your audience and streamline your development process.

MINNA

MINNA — An Online Shopping and E-commerce
=========================================

MINNA is a sleek, modern, and responsive e-commerce website template, designed specifically for fashion and lifestyle brands. With its user-centric design and seamless Shopify integration with the Frameship plugin, MINNA provides everything you need to create.

About this Template
-------------------

🚀 **Transform Your Online Store with MINNA – A Premium E-commerce Template Built on Framer**

**MINNA** is a sleek, modern, responsive e-commerce website template, designed specifically for fashion and lifestyle brands. With its user-centric design and seamless Shopify integration with the Frameship plugin, MINNA provides everything you need to create a visually stunning, conversion-focused online store.

**Key Features:**

*   🎨 **Modern Aesthetic Design**
    
*   📱 **Fully Responsive**
    
*   🛒 **Shopify Integration**
    
*   🚚 **Customer-Friendly Features**
    
*   📧 **Built-In Newsletter Subscription**
    
*   ⚡ **Fast Loading**
    
*   💼 **Customizable for Any Brand**
    

**Perfect For:**

*   Fashion brands
    
*   Lifestyle product stores
    
*   Small businesses and entrepreneurs launching their first online store
    

💡 **Why Choose MINNA?** Stand out from the competition with a premium design that captivates your audience and drives sales. Whether you're a seasoned seller or just starting, MINNA empowers you to build an online store that reflects your brand's excellence.

DISCOUNTS:

*   Use the **ULVIN** promo code for %10 OFF on the **Frameship** plugin
    
*   **PARTNER25PROYEARLY** for 3 months free yearly Pro subscription when upgrading Framer
